\bentry
\word[O(1)]{O}
\pron{O}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{(\eng{o} eMdU \parx) (\bava\ \eng{Os} yA \eng{O's}) 
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya hadineYdaneya akaSxra.
\hypertarget{O(1)2}{}
\num{2} (\eng{o}) (dUravANi saMKeyx \mo\ saMKAyxsherxVNiyalilx, \kanmu\ 
mAtanADuvAga) sonenx; shUnayx.
\num{3} \eng{O} vagaRda rakatx; \eng{ABO} vayxvasethxya
mAnavarakatxda guMpugaLalolxMdu.
\num{4} \eng{`o'} AkArada gurutu.
\num{5} vatuRla; vaqtatx; \kanmu\ guMDAda AkAra.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[O(4)]{O}
\pron{O}
\gl{\BAavayx}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{\hyperlink{oh(1)}{${}^1$oh}} eMba padada rUpAMtara.
\num{2} (saMboVdhaneya hiMde alapxvirAma cihenxyiMda parxteyxVkisadAga
\eng{o} rUpa, parxteyxVkisidAga \eng{oh} rUpa) O! OhoV! ayoyxV!
ababx! \eng{O dear me}! ayoyxV nananx pADeV, goVLeV! \eng{O for a
breathing-space}! O, usirADalu avakAsha sikikxdare! \eng{Oh, what a
lie} ababx, eMtha suLuLx! \eng{Oh, is that so}? OhoV! hAgoV? \eng{O
God}! ayoyxV deVvare! 
\num{3} 
\alnum{a} (\eng{O yes}!) O, Agali! OhoV Agali! 

\alnum{b} \eng{= \hyperlink{oyes}{oyes}.}}

\bentry
\word[oak(1)]{oak}
\pron{Okf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} Okf mara yA pode; kevxkaRsf kulakekx seVrida,
hAlegaLaMtha elegaLuLaLx, haNuNx biDuva oMdu mara yA pode.
\num{2} Okf (marada) dAru; \kanmu\ piVThoVpakaraNa matutx
kaTaTxDagaLalilx baLasuva gaTiTxyAda, belebALuva I marada dAru.
\num{3} (\birx) (\vivi gaLa kAleVjukoThaDigaLa) horabAgilu: \eng{sport
one's oak} BeVTigAraranunx niSeVdhisalu horabAgilu hAku, mucucx.
\hypertarget{oak(1)4}{}
\num{4} (\eng{the Oaks}) (\Eva vAgi baLake) Okf (paMdayx);
iMgelxMDina epasxmf nagaradalilx naDeyuva mUru vaSaR vayasisxna
heNuNxkudure marigaLa jUju.
\num{5} Okf (marada) elegaLu: \eng{ oak is still worn on 29th May} meV
 $29$raMdu IgalU Okf elegaLanunx dharisalAgutatxde.
\num{6} Okf baNaNx; Okf marada eLeyelegaLa baNaNx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{dwarf, ground, etc., oak} Okf maravanunx hoVluva
saNaNx gAtarxda giDagaLu.
\num{2} \eng{dyer's holm, scarlet, etc., oak} vividha jAtiya Okf
maragaLu.
\num{3} \eng{oak-beauty, oak-egger, oak-lappet, oak-hook-tip} Okf
eletiMdu beLeyuva yA Okf elegaLanunx hoVluva bagebageya ciTeTxgaLu.
\num{4} \eng{oak-fig, oak-plum, oak-potato, oak-spangle, oak-wart} Okf
maragaLalilx gAlf phelxY eMba noNagaLiMda Aguva bagebageya
gaMTugaLu. 
\num{5} \eng{the Oaks = \hyperlink{oak(1)4}{${}^1$oak(4)}.}}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[oar(1)]{oar}
\pron{Orf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (doVNi naDesuva) huTuTx; toLe; jalulx; jalelx.
\num{2} aMbiga; huTuTxgAra; huTuTxhAkuvavanu; toLe ocucxvavanu; jalulx
hAkuvavanu.
\num{3} (\rUpa) 

\alnum{a} rekekx.

\alnum{b} Iju rekekx.

\alnum{c} (IjuvAga biVsuva) toVLu itAyxdi.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{chained to the oar} jalelxge kaTiTxhAkida; meY
muriyuvaMtaha hAgU bahu diVGaR avadhiya kelasavanunx niraMtaravAgi
mADabeVkAda nibaRMdhakekx sikikx; doVNige kaTiTxda gulAmanaMte
duDiyuva kaTuTxpADigoLagAgi.
\num{2} \eng{four-oar} nAlukx huTiTxna doVNi.
\num{3} \eng{have an oar in every man's boat} elalxra vayxvahAradalUlx
tale hAku, keYhAku.
\num{4} \eng{lay (\engit{or} lie) on one's oars = \hyperlink{oar1pagu8}{\pagu(8)}.}
\num{5} \eng{pair-oar} joVDi huTiTxna doVNi.
\num{6} \eng{pulls a good oar} oLeLxya huTuTxgAra, aMbiga.
\num{7} \eng{put in one's oars} naDuve talehAku; keYhAku.
\hypertarget{oar1pagu8}{}
\num{8} \eng{rest on one's oars} meYmuriyuvaMtaha duDimeya baLike tusu
hotutx visharxmisu, vishArxMti tegeduko, kelasa nililxsiru.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{oat}
\pron{OTf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} OTf:

\alnum{a} toVke goVdhi; avena sAyxTiva kulakekx seVrida, 
shiVtavalayagaLalilx beLesuva oMdu dhAnayxda giDa yA sasayx.

\alnum{b} (\bava dalilx) ahAravAgi baLasuva, I giDada dhAnayx.

\alnum{c} avena kulakekx seVrida, yAvudeV dhAnayx, \kanmu\ kAdu OTf.
\num{2} (\kAparx). 

\alnum{a} OTf kAMDa; \sA\ haLiLxya yA gArxmiVNa kAvayxdalilx kurubaru
\mo varu koLalAgi baLasuva, oTf giDada kAMDa.

\alnum{b} haLiLxya hADu, kavana; gArxmiVNa kAvayx; gArxma
jiVvanavanunx kurita padayx, kAvayx.
\num{3} (\bava dalilx) (\ashi) leYMgika suKa taqpitx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\hyperdef{O}{oat pagu(1)}{}
\num{1} \eng{feel one's pats} (\AmA) 

\alnum{a} (\ame) tAnobabx parxmuKa vayxkitxyeMdu BAvisiko; tAnobabx
doDaDx vayxkitxyeMdu bAvisiko.

\alnum{b} ulAlxsadiMdiru; utAsxha tuMbiru; caTuvaTikeyiMda koDisu.
\num{2} \eng{off one's oats} (\AmA) hasivilalxdiru; tinanxlu
iceCxyilalxdiru; AhAra beVDadiru.
\hyperdef{O}{oat pagu(3)}{}
\num{3} \eng{sow one's oats (\engit{or} wild oats)} (saMyama, gAMBiVyaRgaLu
sithxragoLuLxva munanx) ywvanada Baradalilx savxcaCxMdavAgi,
setxYravAgi vatiRsu; ywvanadalilx gaMDAgULiyAgiru.
\num{4} \eng{wild oat = \hyperlink{oat-grass}{oat-grass}.}}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{ob-}
\pron{abf-}
\gl{\pUparx}
\dictmeaning{\eng{c} ge hiMde \eng{oc- (occasion)}, \eng{f} ge hiMde \eng{of
(offend) p} ge hiMde \eng{op- (oppose)} rUpAMtara hoMduva, \kanmu\
lAyxTinf mUlada padagaLalilx I athaRgaLalilx parxyoVgavAguva \pUparx:
\num{1} goVcarate; parxkaTavAgiruvike; \eng{object, obnoxious,
obtrude, obverse}.
\num{2} edurAgu; aBumuKavAgu; edurige--kANu, iru, nilulx:
\eng{observe, obvious, opportune}.
\num{3} yAvudeV dikikxnalilx; kaDege: \eng{oblation, oblong, offer}.
\num{4} viroVdha; devxVSa; \eng{objurgate, obloquy, obstreperous,
oppose, oppress, opprobrium}.
\num{5} parxtiroVdha; niroVdhaka; niroVdha; taDe: \eng{obdurate,
obstinate, obtuse}.
\num{6} aDiDx; aDacaNe; mare mADuvike: \eng{obese, obscure,
obstacle, obstruct, occlude, occult, oppilate}. 
\num{7} aMtayx; kone; samApitx; saMpUNaRvAgiruvike: \eng{obsolete,
obtain, occident, occupy}.
\num{8} (Adhunika veYjAcnxnika pAriBASikagaLalilx) vipayaRyavAgi;
parxtiloVmavAgi; vayxtirikatxvAgi;
sAmAnayxvAdudakekx virudadhxvAda dikikxnalilx yA riVtiyalilx:
\eng{obconical, obovate, obcordate}.
\num{9} GaTisu; saMBavisu; saMyoVgadiMda Agu: \eng{occasion, occur,
offend}. 
\num{10} namarxte; vidheVyate: \eng{obey, obsequious}.} 
\eentry

\bentry

\word[oblique(1)]{oblique}
\pron{abfliVkf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} OreyAda; bAgida; parxvaNa: 

\alnum{a} meVlina dikikxniMda yA samataladiMda bAgida .

\alnum{b} neVravAda gereyiMda yA hAdiyiMda beVreyAda dikukx hiDida.
\num{2} sututx baLasina; paroVkaSx vidhAnada; sutitxbaLasi baruva;
neVravAgi viSayakekx hoVgada.
\num{3} (\jAyx) vAlida; bAgida; OreyAda; tiyaRkf:

\alnum{a} (reVKe, samatala, \mo vugaLa \vi) samakoVnadalilxlalxda.

\alnum{b} (koVnada \vi) Ore(yAda); laGu yA vishAlakoVnada.

\alnum{c} (shaMku, uruLe, \mo vugaLa \vi) AdhAratalakekx
laMbavAgilalxda akaSxvuLaLx.
\num{4} vAlida; bAgida; tiyaRkf:

\alnum{a} (\aMrashA) deVhada yA keYkAlugaLa akaSxkekx samAMtaravAgiyAgali
laMbavAgiyAgali ilalxdiruva.

\alnum{b} (\savi) (eleya \vi) eraDu pakakxgaLU samavAgilalxdiruva.
\hypertarget{oblique(1)5}{}
\num{5} (\vAyx) parxthamA saMboVdhana Binanx viBakitxya; parxthamA,
saMboVdhana viBakitxgaLanunx biTuTx uLida viBakitxgaLanunx sUcisuva,
toVrisuva.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{oblique case = \hyperlink{oblique(1)5}{${}^1$oblique(5)}.}
\num{2} \eng{oblique narration} paroVkaSx kathana; sututxbaLasina
kathana, nirUpaNe.}
\eentry

\num{3} \eng{fall into oblivion}

\alnum{a} visamxqqtavAgu, mareyalapxDu; (janara) visamxqqtigoLagAgu.

\alnum{b} gatapArxyavAgu; baLakeyalilxlalxde hoVgu.}

\bentry
\word{observance}
\pron{abfsazvaRnfsx}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} (shAsana, kataRvayx, padadhxti, matiVya kaTaTxLe,
vidhi, AcaraNe, \mo vugaLa) AcaraNe; pAlane; anusaraNe; anuSAThxna.
\num{2} (dhAmiRkavAda yA shAsotxrXVkatxvAda) kamARcaraNe; matAcAra;
sAMparxdAyika kamARnuSAThxna.

saMparxdAya.

\bentry
\word[occasion(1)]{occasion}
\pron{akeVSaz(Sfz)nf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} 
\alnum{a} visheVSa--GaTane, saMdaBaR; visheVSavAda yA
gamanAhaRvAda--parisithxti, saMdaBaR: \eng{dressed for the
occasion} saMdaBaRkekx takakxMte veVSa toTaTx; saMdaBoRVcitavAda
poVSAku dharisida.
\eng{on this festive occasion} I utasxva saMdaBaRdalilx.

\alnum{b} visheVSa samaya, saMdaBaR; visheVSa saMgati yA GaTane
naDeyuva nidiRSaTx samaya: \eng{on the occasion of 
their marriage} maduveya samayadalilx, saMdaBaRdalilx.
\num{2} kAraNa; samathaRne; AdhAra: \eng{ there is no occasion to be
angry} koVpisikoLaLxlu kAraNaveVnU ilalx.
\num{3} susamaya; susaMdaBaR; sadavakAsha; yAvudeV kelasa mADalu
takakx--samaya, saMdaBaR, avakAsha: \eng{take occasion} (mADalu)
avakAshavanunx paDeduko, upayoVgisiko.
\num{4} gwNa, pArxsaMgika--kAraNa; sadayxH kAraNa; tatfkaSxNada,
Adare gwNavAda yA pArxsaMgikavAda kAraNa: \eng{the cause of revolution
may be obscure while its occasion is obvious} kArxMtiya pArxsaMgika
kAraNa sapxSaTxvAgidadxrU adara mUla kAraNavu gUDhavAgirabahudu.
\eng{the assassination was the occasion of the war} KUniyu yudadhxkekx
pArxsaMgika kAraNavAgitutx.
\num{5} perxVraka (kAraNa); perxVraNe: \eng{gave occasion to a burst
of laughter} goLeLxMdu nagalu kAraNavAyitu.
\num{6} agatayx; Avashayxkate: \eng{the Queen has no occasion for the
services of the officer} rANiyavarige (I) adhikAriya seVveya
agatayxvilalx (avananunx vajA mADalu baLasuva swmayx sUtarx).
\num{7} (\bava dalilx) vayxvahAragaLu; kelasakAyaRgaLu; vaqtitxge
saMbaMdhisida kAyaRkalApagaLu: \eng{ go about one's lawful occasions}
tananx nAyxyabadadhx vayxvahAragaLalilx niratanAgiru; tanage
saMbaMdhisida kelasa kAyaRgaLanunx mADutitxru.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{celebrate the occasion} saMdaBaRvanunx
utasxvarUpadalilx Acarisu.
\num{2} \eng{rise to the occasion} asAdhAraNa saMdaBaRvodagidAga
adakekx takakx yA agatayxvAda icAcxshakitx, bala, sAmathayxR, \mo
vanunx toVrisu, parxdashiRsu.

\bentry
\word{octopus}
\pron{AkaTxpasf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{(\bava\ \eng{octopuses}). 
\num{1} AkaTxpasf; aSaTxpAdi:

\alnum{a} bAyiya sutatxlU cUSAmxMgagaLuLaLx eMTu udadxvAda
bAhugaLiruva; AkaTxpoDa gaNakekx seVrida maqduvAda ciVladaMtha
deVhavuLaLx, balavAda kokikxnaMtha davaDegaLuLaLx, apAyakAriyAda,
shiVSaRpAdi kaDalajiVvigaLa kula. \quad
\hyperlink{Octopus-1figure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage
width 0.6cm height 0.5cm {O_Pictures/Octopus-1.jpg}}}

\alnum{b} I kulakekx seVrida shiVSaRpAdi cipupxjiVvi, maqdavxMgi
\num{2} saMhatAdhikAra yA saMGaTita parxBAva; saMGaTitavAda,
bahumuKavAda, \sA\ hAnikaravAda--adhikAra yA parxBAva.}

\bentry
\word[odd(1)]{odd}
\pron{ADf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} vicitarxvAda; vilakaSxNavAda; vakarxvAda; acacxriya;
acacxri huTiTxsuvaMtha; asAmanayxvAda; asAdhAraNavAda; sAmAnayx riVti
biTuTx tananxdeV Ada riVtiyuLaLx: \eng{oddest creature I have ever
seen} nAnu noVDiruvavaralelxlalx atayxMta vicitarx pArxNi.
\num{2} aniyata; niyatavalalxda; anishicxta; sAMdaBiRka
; gotutxvaLiyilalxda: \eng{picks up odd jobs} yAvudoV aniyata
kelasagaLanunx saMpAdisikoLuLxtAtxne.
\num{3} sAmAnayxvAgi yArU gamanisada yA parigaNisada: \eng{in some odd
corner} yArU gamanisada oMdu mUleyalilx. \eng{picks up odd bargains}
elolxV mUleyalilxruva agagxda sarakanunx koLuLxtAtxne.
\num{4} biDuvina; kelasavilalxda: \eng{odd moments} biDuvina,
kaSxNagaLu, kAla.
\num{5} UhisalAgada; necicxkeyilalxda; anishicxta.
\num{6} hecicxgeya; adhika; lekakxkikxMta hecicxna: \eng{swept up the
odd bits left on the floor} nelada meVle uLididadx hecicxna
cUrugaLanunx guDisi etitxkoMDa. \eng{earned the odd rupee} mAmUligiMta
hecicxna rUpAyiyanunx gaLisida.
\num{7} 
\alnum{a} ($3, 5$ \mo vugaLaMtha saMKeyxgaLa \vi) besa; viSama; migilu;
eraDu sama saMKeyxya guMpAgi viBAgisida meVle uLida yA eraDariMda
nisheshxVSavAgi BAgavAgada.

\alnum{b} (anukarxmavAgi eNike mADuvaMte joVDisiruva vasutxgaLalilx yA
vayxkitxgaLalilx) besa saMKeyxya; viSama aMkeya: \eng{no parking on
odd dates} besasaMKeyxya dinagaLalilx vAhanagaLa nilugaDe ilalx.
\num{8} (itara elalxvanUnx vitaraNe mADida naMtara ilalxve joVDigaLAgi
viBAgisida naMtarada) sheVSa; uLikeya; uLida: \eng{have got an odd
sock} oMdu kAluciVla uLidide.
\num{9} (niyata kAlikegaLu, garxMthamAle, \mo vugaLa \vi) biDi;
karxmavilalxda; saMbaMdhavilalxda; oMdu sherxVNi yA oMdu vagaRdiMda
beVreyAgiruva: \eng{a few odd volumes} kelavu biDi saMpuTagaLu.
\eng{odd numbers} (sherxVNige karxma badadhxvAgi seVrada) biDi
saMcikegaLu.
\num{10} (saMKeyx, motatx, tUka, \mo vugaLa sUcayx padakekx
seVrisidAga) -kikxMta savxlapx hecicxna; adhika cilalxreya: \eng{forty
odd} nalavatUtx cilalxre; nalavatatxra meVle aivatatxroLage.
\eng{sixty thousand odd} aruvatutx sAvira matutx kelavu nUrugaLu,
hatutxgaLu yA biDigaLu. 
\eng{sixty odd thousand} aruvatutx cilalxre sAvira; aruvatutx sAvirada
meVle epapxtutx sAvirada oLage. \eng{forty-odd people} nalavatutx
cilalxre janagaLu; nalavatatxkikxMta hecucx, aivatatxkikxMta kaDame
jana.
\num{11} hecacxLa; uLike; meVlina cilalxreya; pUNaR saMKeyxgiMta yA
hesarisida mobalagigiMta eSuTx hecocxV aSaTxra: \eng{here is a
ten-rupee note; pay the bill and keep the odd money} igoV I hatutx
rUpAyina noVTu tegeduko; bilalxnunx pAvati mADi uLikeyanunx,
hecicxnadanunx, cilalxreyanunx niVneV iTuTxko. \eng{we have 102; what
shall we do with the odd 2}? namamx hatitxra $102$ ide. I cilalxre
eraDanunx Enu mADoVNa? }}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{odd and even} sari besa yA sarimigilu ATa.
\num{2} \eng{the odd man} besa saMKeyxya sadasayxriruva samiti \mo
vugaLalilx niNARyakavAda voVTu koDuvavanu; niNARyaka matadAra.
\num{3} \eng{the odd man out}

\alnum{a} nANayx miDidu mUvaralilx obabxnanunx mAtarx Ayudx koLuLxva
vidhAna, upAya.

\alnum{b} vilakaSxNa vayxkitx yA vasutx; yAvudAdaroMdu viSayadalilx
oMdu taMDadalilx itara vayxkitxgaLu yA vasutxgaLigiMta beVreyAgiruva
vayxkitx yA vasutx.
\num{4} \eng{the odd trick} (visfTx isipxVTATadalilx eraDu pakaSxgaLU
ArAru paTuTxgaLanunx paDeda meVle uLida) hadimUraneya paTuTx.}

\bentry
\word{odds}
\pron{ADf\char144}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{(\bava) 
\num{1} (eraDU kaDegU iruva niriVkiSxta saMBAvayxteyanunx avalaMbisi,
paMthagAraru oDuDxva) paNada anupAta yA adara parxmANa: \eng{give (or
lay) odds of three to one} oMdakekx mUraraSuTx (paNa) oDuDx.
\num{2} hecucx saMBava; adhika saMBAvayxte; yAvudeV pariNAma Aguva
asaMBavaniVyategiMta iruva hecicxna saMBavaniVyate: \eng{the odds are
that he will do it} avanu adanunx mADuva saMBavaveV hecucx: \eng{the
odds are that it will rain} maLeyAguva saMBavaveV hecucx.
\num{3} parxtikUlakikxMta hecicxna anukUla; \eng{the odds are in oue
favour} namage parxtikUlaveV hecAcxgide. \eng{I have fought against
longer odds} idakikxMta hecicxna parxtikUlagaLanunx edurisidedxVne
(eMdare Iga parxtikUla aSeTxVnU hecicxlalx), \eng{won the against all
the adds} elalx parxtikUlagaLidadxrU, elalx parxtikUlagaLa virudadhx
gedadx. \eng{the adds are against him} avanu gelulxva sAdhayxte
kaDame.
\num{4} (sapxdhiRgaLalilx dubaRlanAdavanige itararoDane sama avakAsha
kalipxsikoDalu niVDuva) riyAyiti: \eng{give adds}(dubaRla
sapxdhiRge) riyAyiti niVDi samAvakAsha kalipxsikoDu.
\num{5} (anukUlakara) vayxtAyxsa: \eng{what is the adds}? adariMdeVnu?
adariMdeVnu toMdare? \eng{it makes no adds} adariMda EnU vayxtAyxsavAgadu.
\num{6} (\pArxparx) hecucxkaDame; veYSamayx; asamate: \eng{make adds
even} hecucx kaDime ilalxdaMte mADu; sarisama mADu.
\num{7} viroVdha; hoVrATa; parxtikUla: \eng{they are at adds with
fate} avaru vidhiyoDane, adaqSaTxdoDane hoVrADutitxdAdxre.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{at adds}

\alnum{a} virudadxvAgi.

\alnum{b} asamaMjasavAgi; hoMdANikeyilalxde.
\num{2} \eng{by all adds} KaMDitavAgi; nishacxyavAgi.
\num{3} \eng{adds and ends} cUrupAru; uLikepaLike; cilalxrepalalxre.
\num{4} \eng{over the adds} oTiTxnalilx opipxda bele \mo vugaLigiMta 
hecAcxgi.
\num{5} \eng{take adds} inonxbabxnige ananukUlavAguvaMte paNavoDuDx;
inonxbabxnigiMta kaDame paNavoDuDx.}

\bentry
\word{of}
\pron{Avf, avf}
\gl{\upa}
{\dictmeaning{I keLage vagiRVkarisiruvaMte, adara muMdina nAmapadavanunx (yA
savaRnAmavanunx) hiMde baMdiruva nAmapada, visheVSaNa,
kirxyAvisheVSaNa yA kirxyApadakekx anavxyisi avugaLa saMbaMdhagaLanunx
sUcisuva upasagaR parxyoVgada saMdaBaRgaLu: 
\num{1}
\alnum{a} huTuTx; mUla; ugama sAthxna: \eng{be of} vaMshadavanAgiru.
\eng{come of descend of} vaMshadalilx huTiTxru. \eng{spring of ...}
iMda huTuTx, udaBxvisu.

\alnum{b} (vayxkitx \mo variMda) baMdadudx; paDedadudx: \eng{borrow
of} sAla tegeduko. \eng{buy of} (obabxniMda) koMDuko. \eng{win of}
(obabxniMda) gedudxko.
\eng{receive of} koDugeyAgi tegeduko; koTaTxdadxnunx
sivxVkarisu. \eng{hire of} bADigege tegeduko.

\alnum{c} kAraNa; heVtu; kAraka shakitx; perxVraka (vayxkitx yA mUla):
\eng{die of} (roVga \mo vugaLiMda) sAyu. \eng{sick of measles}
daDAradiMda hAsige hiDidu. \eng{sick of delays} viLaMbadiMda
beVsaravuMTAgi.
\eng{warned of God} deVvariMdaleV ecacxrisalapxTuTx, ecacxrike paDedu.

\alnum{d} kataqR; yAvudanenxV mADuvavanu yA uMTumADuvavanu:
\eng{paintings of Ravivarma} ravivamaR racisida, ravivamaRna
vaNaRcitarxgaLu. 
\num{2} (oMdu vasutx \mo vu yAvudariMda racitavAgideyoV A) sAmagirx;
darxvayx: \eng{built of brick} iTiTxgeyiMda kaTiTxda. \eng{house of
cards} isipxVTelegaLiMda nimiRsida mane. 
\eng{a family of eight} eMTu janaruLaLx yA janariMda kUDida kuTuMba.
\num{3} (obabxnige, oMdakekx iruva) saMbaMdhada; seVrida;
saMbaMdhisida; sAvxmayxda: \eng{we, of the middle class} madhayxma
vagaRkekx seVrida nAvu. \eng{companions of his exile} avana
deVshaBarxSaTxteya (kAlada) oDanADigaLu.
\eng{articles of clothing} uDugetoDugegaLa halavu vasutxgaLu. 
\eng{the manners of today} iMdina riVtiniVtigaLu. 
\eng{a thing of the past} gatakAlada--vasutx, viSaya. \eng{the
master of the house} maneya yajamAna .
\eng{the widow of the man who was killed} hatanAdavana vidhave.
\eng{a topic of conversation} saMBASaNeya oMdu viSaya.
\num{4} (tAdAtamxyX yA nikaTa saMbaMdha): \eng{the class of idiots}
mUKaR vagaR. \eng{a fool of a man} mUKaR manuSayx. \eng{her scamp of a
husband} avaLa gaMDanenisikoMDiruva ayoVgayx. \eng{the worst liar of
any man I know} nanage tiLidiruvavaralelxlalx atayxMta suLuLxgAra.
\eng{I had a bad time of it} adu nanage tuMbA kaSaTx koTiTxtu.
\eng{I had a troublesome journey of it} adu nanage tiVra toMdareya
parxyANavAgitutx. 
\eng{the city of Rome} roVmf (eMba) nagara. \eng{the
vice of drunkenness} kuDukutanada cALi.
\eng{a kilogram of apples} oMdu kiloV seVbu.
\num{5} (saMbaMdhavanunx) kaLedu koLuLxvudu; tapipxsikoLuLxvudu;
nivArisikoLuLxvudu; pariharisikoLuLxvudu: \eng{heal of} (roVga \mo
vanunx) pariharisiko. \eng{rid of}, nivArisiko. \eng{ease of}
(kaLedukoLuLxvudara mUlaka) sarAga mADiko.
\num{6} (saMbaMdha) ilalxdiruvudu; (saMbaMdhada) rAhitayx; aBAva:
\eng{destitute of} (yAvudeV vasutx yA EnoV) ilalxdiru. \eng{empty
of} (EnU ilalxde) KAliyagi. \eng{free of} vimukatxvAgi.
\eng{bare of} shUnayxvAgi; rahitavAgi.

dUradalilxruvudu: \eng{north of} utatxradalilx; utatxrakekx,

biTuTxhoVgu: \eng{take leave of} agali hoVgu; biVLokxLuLx; biVLokxMDu
hoVgu.
\num{9} (saMbaMdha) tapipxsuvudu; toreyuvudu: \eng{baulk of} (yAvudeV
vasutx \mo vu sikakxdaMte) tapipxsu; aDiDx paDisu; taDe. \eng{cheat,

\num{10} (nideRVshisida yA sUcayxvAgiruva) saMbaMdha ilalxdiruvudu:
\eng{independently of} Ashirxta saMbaMdhavilalxde; savxtaMtarxvAgi.
\eng{guiltless of} aparAdha ilalxdiru; niraparAdhiyAgiru; aparAdha
vimukatxnAgiru. \eng{irrespective of} gaNanege tegedukoLaLxde;
lekikxsade; nirapeVkeSxvAgi.

saMbaMdhada.

\bentry
\word[oil(1)]{oil}
\pron{Ailf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} eNeNx; teYla; niVrinalilx karagada, niVrina meVle
teVluva, AlakxhAlf, Itharf, beni\char144Vnf, \mo\ kAbaRnika dArxvakagaLalilx
karaguva, jiDuDx savxBAvada, rAsAyanikavAgi taTasathx guNada,
uriyabalalx darxva padAthaR yA sulaBavAgi darxvavAguva Gana padAthaR.
\num{2} (\ame) \eng{= \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{petroleum}{petroleum}.}
\num{3} (\saMpa gaLalilx) iMdhana; iMdhanavAgi baLasuva eNeNx:
\eng{oil-lamp} eNeNxdiVpa.
\num{4} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) 

\alnum{a} \eng{= \hyperlink{oil-paint}{oil-paint}.}

\alnum{b} (\AmA) teYla vaNaRcitarx; teYla vaNaRcitarxgaLanunx baLasi
racisida citarx: \eng{his best oils are exhibited here} ililx Atana
atuyxtatxma teYla vaNaRcitarxgaLanunx parxdashiRsalAgide.
\num{5} (\bava dalilx) \eng{= \hyperlink{oilskin}{oilskin}.}
\num{6} beNeNxmAtu; muKasutxti mADuva, pusalAyisuva mAtu.
\num{7} (\AseTxrXV\ matutx nUyxsizVlaMDf) 

\alnum{a} sudidx; samAcAra.

\alnum{b} saMgatigaLu; nijAMshagaLu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\hyperdef{O}{oil(1) pagu(1)}{}
\num{1} \eng{burn the midnight oil} rAtirx bahaLa
hotitxnavaregU Odu yA kelasa mADu.
\num{2} \eng{drying oil} Aruva eNeNx; oNaguva eNeNx; gALigoDiDxdAga
oNaguva eNeNx; vAyuvina kirxyeyiMda gaTiTxyAguva, AdudariMda
oNagidaMtAguva, kelavu bageya biVjagaLiMda tegeda
AviyAguvaMthadalalxda yAvudeV eNeNx, \udA\ agase eNeNx.
\num{3} \eng{non-drying oil} Arada eNeNx; Ganisada eNeNx; vAyuvina
kirxyeyiMda gaTiTxyAgada yAvudeV kobebxNeNx.
\num{4} \eng{oil and vinegar (\engit{or} water)} eNeNx siVgekAyi; parasapxra
virudadhxvAdavu.
\num{5} \eng{oil of almonds} bAdAmi eNeNx; bAdAmi biVjadiMda tegeda
eNeNx.
\num{6} \eng{oil of vitriol = \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{sulphuric acid}{sulphuric acid}.}
\num{7} \eng{pour oil on the flame} uriyuva beMkige tupapx suri;
parisithxtiyanunx ulbxNisu.
\num{8} \eng{pour oil on the water} shamana mADu; samAdhAna mADu;
sAMtavxnagoLisu.
\num{9} \eng{salad oil} salADf eNeNx; salADf tayArisalu baLasuva
eLeLxNeNxyaMtha yAvudeV eNeNx.
\num{10} \eng{show smell of oil} (parxtiBegiMta hecAcxgi) sharxmada yA
duDimeya cihenx toVru.
\num{11} \eng{strap oil} beliTxniMda bArisu, hoDe.
\num{12} \eng{strike oil} 

\alnum{a} (eNeNxgAgi bAvi koredAga sudeYvadiMda) eNeNx paDe.

\alnum{b} adaqSaTxshAliyAgi aishavxyaRgaLisu, yashasusx paDe.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[old(1)]{old}
\pron{OlfDx}
\gl{\gu} (\tara\ \eng{older}, \tama\ \eng{oldest}). 
{\dictmeaning{(visheVSAthaRgaLalilx \eng{elder, eldest}).
\num{1} 
\alnum{a} vayasAsxda; mudi; mupipxna; vaqdadhx.

\alnum{b} vayasAsxda; cikakxdalalxda yA adara AraMBa dasheyalilalxda.
\num{2} haLeya; haLatAda; hiMdeMdoV tayArAda, racisida: \eng{old book}
haLeya pusatxka.
\num{3} haLeya; bahaLa kAladiMda baLakeyalilxruva, baLasiruva:
\eng{old suit} haLeya sUTu.
\num{4} haLeya(dAda); upayoVgavaLida; (upayoVgisidudariMda)
shithilavAda; jiVNaRvAda: \eng{old clothes} haLeya baTeTxgaLu.
\num{5} vayasAsxda; mudi; vaqdadhx; vayasAsxda lakaSxNa, vayasisxna
anuBava dwbaRlayx, \mo vugaLanunxLaLx: \eng{the child has an old face}
maguvige vayasAsxdaMte kANuva muKavide.
\num{6} haLeya; nurita; paLagida; anuBavi; anuBava paDeda: \eng{old in
cunning} kapaTadalilx nuritavanu, paLagidavanu. \eng{an old offender}
haLeya, paLagida aparAdhi. \eng{old in crime} aparAdhadalilx nurita.
\num{7} haLeya kAlakekx seVrida; gatakAlada: \eng{old times} haLeya
dinagaLu; gatakAla. \eng{haunted by old memories} gatakAlada
nenapugaLa giVLu kADuva.
\num{8} bahaLa hiMdina; haLegAlada; purAtana; pArxciVna; tiVra haLeya
kAlada: \eng{old as the hills} girigaLaSuTx pArxciVnavAda. \eng{old
friends} haLeya geLeyaru. \eng{an old family} hiMdiniMda
parxsidadhxvAda, purAtanavAda vaMsha, kula.
\num{9} (oMdu gotAtxda) vayasisxna; nidiRSaTx vayasisxna: \eng{is four
years old} nAlukx vaSaR vayasAsxgide. \eng{a four-year-old boy}
nAlukx vaSaR vayasisxna huDuga.
\num{10} (BASeya \vi) haLeya; pArxciVna; purAtana.
\num{11} (\AmA) haLeya; pirxya; pirxVtiyiMda (yA saligeyiMda) yA
anwpacArikavAgi kareyuvAga \parx: \eng{good old Charlie} haLeya pirxya
caliR.
\num{12} haLeya; hiMdina; eraDaralilx modalaneya yA aneVka
vasutxgaLalilx modalaneya: \eng{our old house} namamx haLeya
mane. \eng{wants his old job back} tananx haLeya, hiMdina kelasavanunx
apeVkiSxsutAtxne.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{an old name} pArxciVnanAma; hiMdiniMda
parxsidadhxvAda hesaru.
\num{2} \eng{any old thing} (\ashi) eMthadoV oMdu; yAvudAdarU sari.
\num{3} \eng{call up old memories} haLeya nenapugaLanunx jAcnxpakakekx
taru, samxrisu.
\num{4} \eng{four etc. -year-old} nAlukx \mo\ vayasisxna vayxkitx,
pArxNi (\kanmu\ A vayasisxna jUju kudure).
\num{5} \eng{good old} haLeya vayxkitxya yA vasutxvina viSayavAgi
nijavAda yA avana yA adara hesarinoDane \parx: \eng{good old uncle}
namamx haLeya doDaDxpapx.
\num{6} \eng{of old standing} bahaLa kAlada; lAgAyatiniMda iruva;
diVGaRsAthxpita; bahaLa hiMdina kAladiMdalU iruva.
\hypertarget{oldpagu7}{}
\num{7} \eng{old chap, fellow, son, etc.,} pirxVti yA saligeyiMda
gaMDasu yA gaMDu pArxNiyanunx saMboVdhisuvAga baLasuva padagucaCx.
\num{8} \eng{old countries} haLenADugaLu; purAtana deVshagaLu; bahu
hiMdiniMda janaru vAsavAgiruva yA nAgarikavAgiruva deVshagaLu.
\num{9} \eng{Old Harry, Nick, Scratch} seYtAna.
\num{10} \eng{old London, Paris, England, etc.,}

\alnum{a} purAtana, pArxciVna--laMDanf, pAyxrisf, iMgelxMDf, \mo vu.

\alnum{b} (laMDanf \mo\ nagaragaLa) purAtana avasheVSagaLu.
\num{11} \eng{old ocean} anAdikAlada samudarx.
\num{12} \eng{old red sandstone} birxTaninxnalilx dorakuva DevoVniyanf
kAlada keMpu maraLugalulx.
\num{13} \eng{old scores}

\alnum{a} haLeya lekakx.

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) haLeya seVDu: \eng{pay off old scores} haLeya seVDu
tiVrisiko.
\num{14} \eng{old thing, fruit, top, etc.,} (\ashi) =
\hyperlink{oldpagu7}{\pagu $(7)$}. 
\num{15} \eng{the old} 

\alnum{a} haLeyadu; hosatalalxdudx.

\alnum{b} vayasAsxdavaru; mudukaru; vaqdadhxru.
\num{16} \eng{the old country} (valasegAraru, nelasunADinavaru, \mo

savxdeVsha.
\num{17} \eng{the old changeth} haLeya saMparxdAyagaLu mApaRDutatxve.
\num{18} \eng{the yound and old} AbAlavaqdadhxru; elalxrU.
\num{19} \eng{a man is as old as he feels} manasisxge anisidaSuTx
obabxna pArxya; namage eSuTx vayasAsxgide eMdu aMdu koLuLxtetxVveyoV
namage aSeTxV vayasusx; manoVBAvanege takakxMte manuSayxna vayasusx.
\num{20} \eng{an old one} elalxrigU tiLidiruva caTAki, hAsoyxVkitx.
\num{21} \eng{have a fine, good, high, etc., old time} (\ashi)
cenAnxgi moVjumADu; KuSipaDu; suKa, saMtoVSa anuBavisu; majAmADu.
\num{22} \eng{little old} (\ame) (vayxkitx yA vasutxvanunx
pirxVtiyiMda yA tamASeyiMda mAtanADisuvAga baLasuva pada).
\num{23} \eng{my old bones} mudukanAda nAnu, nananxnunx.
\num{24} \eng{old head on young shoulders} vayoVvaqdadxnalalxdidadxrU
jAcnxnavaqdadhx; eLeya vayasAsxdarU beLeda budidhxyavanu.
\hyperdef{O}{old(1) pagu(25)}{}
\num{25} \eng{old wives' tale} muduki kate; ajijxkate; goDuDx
padadhxti yA naMbike; daDaDxtanada yA aveYjAcnxnikavAda saMparxdAya
athavA naMbike.

kaLeyutatx baMdide.

\bentry
\word[olive(1)]{olive}
\pron{Alivf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{Alivf:

\hypertarget{olive(1)a}{}
\alnum{a} Alivf mara; Oliya kulakekx seVrida, kaDuhasiru baNaNxda
BalelxyAkArada togalinaMtidudx, keLaBAgadalilx biLupAgiruva
elegaLuLaLx, \kanmu\ meDiTareVniyanf parxdeVshada Aliya yUroVpiya
matutx dakiSxNa Aphirxkada Aliya AphirxkAna kulagaLige seVrida,
nitayx haridavxNaRda yAvudeV mara. \qquad
\hyperlink{olive-afigure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width
0.5cm height 0.5cm {O_Pictures/olive-a.jpg}}}

\alnum{b} Alivf haNuNx; gaDusAda biVja matutx adanAnxvarisida
maqduvAda kahi tiruLiruva haNuNx biDuva, mAgilalxdAga hasurAgiyU
mAgida meVle niVli kapupx baNaNxdAdxgiyU iruva, aMDAkArada cikakx
haNuNx.
\hypertarget{olive(1)c}{}

\alnum{c} Alivf baNaNx; pakavxvAgada Alivf haNiNxna nasu bUdu hasuru
baNaNx.
\hypertarget{olive(1)d}{}

\alnum{d} Alivf (marada) dAru.

\alnum{e} (\aMrashA) Alivf Utaka; himimxduLina (\eng{medula
oblongata})lilxruva Alivf kAyiya AkArada ububx gubuTugaLeraDaralilx
oMdu.

\alnum{f} (\pArxvi) Aliva kulakekx seVrida, alivf haNiNxna AkArada
udarapadi maqdavxMgi yA I maqdavxMgiya cipupx.

\alnum{g} (danada yA karuvina) mAMsada cUru \mo vugaLanunx Alivf kAyina
AkAradalilx suruLi mADi beVyisida BakaSxyX.

\alnum{h} (shAMti saMdhAna sUcakavAgi) Alivf--ele, koMbe , elegaLa
daMDe.
\hypertarget{olive(1)i}{}

\alnum{i} Alivf kAyina AkArada (adakekx javAbAda inonxMdu
kuNikeyoLakekx hAki uDupanunx BadarxpaDisuva) guMDi \mo\ sAdhana.}

\bentry

\pron{Anf}
\gl{\upa}
{\dictmeaning{(\pagu gaLalilx \eng{upon} eMbudara baLake hecucx).
\num{1} meVle; meVlagxDe; upari; oMdakekx tagulidaMte, adara meVle yA

uMguragaLu. \eng{leaned on his elbow} moNakeY meVle UrikoMDa.

you}? ninanx hatitxra oMdu penfnx ideye?

\eng{I saw them on my return} vApasAda kUDaleV avaranunx noVDide.

oMdu aKaMDa, pUNaR vasutx.}}

\word{oner}
\pron{vanarf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{(\birx) (\ashi)
\num{1} oMdu pwMDu (haNa).
\num{2} asAdhAraNa, adivxtiVya vayxkitx yA vasutx; loVkoVtatxra
(puruSa, vasutx): \eng{a oner at} (\ashi) (yAvudeV viSayadalilx)
nipuNa, parxviVNa, catura, paTu.
\num{3} BAriV--hoDeta, peTuTx, ETu: \eng{gave him a oner} koTeTx
avanigoMdu; oMdu BAriV hoDeta koTeTx avanige.
\num{4} BAriV suLuLx.
\num{5} (\AmA) (\kanmu\ kirxkeTfnalilx) oMdu raninxna hoDeta.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{oneself}
\pron{vanfself\char143}
\gl{\sanA}
\dictmeaning{\eng{one} eMba anideRVshaka savaRnAmada 

\alnum{a} (AtAmxthaRka rUpa) tananxnenx; tanageV: \eng{one must not
deceive oneself} yAvaneV Agali tananxnenxV vaMcisikoLaLxbAradu.
\eng{one must not grab everything for oneself} yAreV Agali elalxvanUnx
tanageV doVcikoLaLxbAradu.

\alnum{b} (avadhAraNAthaRka rUpa) tAneV; tAnAgiyeV; tAnobabxneV(LeV):
\eng{one must do one's work oneself} yAreV Agali tananx savxMta
kelasavanunx tAneV mADikoLaLxbeVku.
\eng{must do one's portion all by oneself} yAreV Agali tananx pAlina
kelasavanunx tAneV mADabeVku.}
\eentry

anAyxyavAda --tiVpuR.
\num{2} oMdu kaDe mAtarx iruva yA naDeyuva.
\num{3} oMdeV kaDe doDaDxdAda; oMdu kaDe yA pakakx inonxMdu kaDegiMta
yA pakakxkikxMta doDaDxdAda.
\num{4} omomxgada; omamxgugxlina; EkapAshavxRda; oMdu muKada: \eng{a
one-sided street} omomxgada biVdi; oMdeV sAlu manegaLiruva
biVdi. \eng{a one-sided plant} (elegaLu yA hUvugaLu kAMDada oMdeV

\bentry
\word[only(1)]{only}
\pron{Onfli}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} keVvala; mAtarx; aSeTxV; baride; sumamxne: \eng{only you can
guess} niVnobabxneV, niVnobabx mAtarx, adanunx Uhisabalelx. \eng{I
only thought I would do it} adanunx mADabeVkeMdu nAnu sumamxne, baride
yoVciside, aSeTx. \eng{I not only heard it but I saw it} nAnadanunx
keVLidadxSeTxV alalx, noVDiyU noVDide. \eng{will only make matters
worse} parisithxtiyanunx matatxSuTx hadageDisutatxde,
aSeTx. \eng{needed six runs only} keVvala Aru ranunxgaLu
beVkitutx. \eng{is only a child} keVvala magu. 
\num{2} AgatAneV; AgaSeTxV; Aga mAtarx; hiMde Agirade: \eng{saw them
only yesterday} avaranunx keVvala ninenx noVDide, ninenxyaSeTxV
noVDide (hiMde alalx).
\num{3} alilxyavarege, muMce--alalxde; -neV; -veV: \eng{arrives only
on Tuesday} maMgaLavAraveV baruvudu (adakekx muMce alalx).
\num{4} keVvala; adakikxMta hecicxna parxyoVjanavilalxde: \eng{hurried
home only to find her gone} avaLu horaTu hoVgidadxnunx
kaMDukoLaLxlaSeTxV manage beVga hoVgidAdxyitu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{if only} hAge, aSuTx--mAtarx, AgibiTaTxre: \eng{if only
someone would leave me a legacy} yArAdarU nanagoMdu Asitx biTuTx
hoVguvudAdare.
\num{2} \eng{only not} aSuTx yA hAge mAtarx Agalilalx; adoMdu mAtarx
Agalilalx; aSuTx mAtarx biTuTx: \eng{he was about to swoon, only he
did not} avanu inenxVnu mUCeR hoVguvudaralilxdadx, Adare hoVgalilalx.
\num{3} \eng{only too} bahaLa; ati; tiVra: \eng{only too glad}
(niriVkiSxsidadxkekx yA iciCxsidadxkekx vayxtirikatxvAgi) bahaLa
saMtoVSa. \eng{only too true} tiVra nija.}
\eentry

\num{3} (Dababx, dhAraka, \mo vugaLa \vi) mucicxlalxda; terediruva;
mucacxLa hAkada. 
\num{4} tereda; mare tegediruva; mucicxlalxda; anAvaqta: \eng{open

\num{5} (ATa) (goVlina bAyi yA itara AkarxmaNada vasutxvina \vi)
arakiSxta; AkarxmaNakekx tutAtxguva.
\num{6} mucucxmareyilalxda; parxkaTa; bahiraMga: \eng{open contempt}
bahiraMga tirasAkxra. \eng{open scandal} bahiraMga pukAru. \eng{open
hostilities} parxkaTa hoVrATagaLu, kadanagaLu.
\num{7} tereda; bicicxda; haraDida; haraDikoMDiruva; haraDiruva:
\eng{open book} tereda pusatxka. 
\eng{had the map open on the table} meVjina meVle BUpaTavanunx
terediTiTxdadx, bicicxTaTx.
\num{8} (baTeTxya \vi) otAtxgilalxda, jALAgiruva; naDuve aMtaragaLiruva.
\num{9} (vayxkitxya \vi) mucucxmareyilalxde; bicucx manasisxna; saraLa
haqdayada; tereda manasisxna; BAvanegaLanunx itararige tiLisabayasuva. 
\num{10} (manasisxna \vi) tereda; mukatx; hosaBAvagaLige tereda;

perxVkaSxkarige teredide. \eng{shop is open at such hours} iMtha
gaMTegaLalilx aMgaDi teredirutatxde.
\num{13} (saBeya \vi) mukatx; sAvaRjanika; savaRrigU parxveVshaviruva;
elalxrigU parxveVshAvakAshaviruva; keVvala sadasayxrU \mo varige
siVmitavAgirade elalxrU barabahudAda.

elalxrigU avakAshaviruva sapxdheRyalilx gedudx gaLisuva
vidAyxthiRveVtana. \eng{race is open to all}

\alnum{b} (kirxVDApaTu, vidAyxthiR, \mo vara \vi) mukatx

\bentry

\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} aBipArxya: \eng{in my opinion} nananx aBipArxyadalilx; nanage toVruvudaralilx.
\num{2} sadayxda naMbike: \eng{am of opinion that} I riVtiyAgi sadayxdalilx naMbidedxVne.
\num{3} eNike; toVcike; anisike.
\num{4} janABipArxya; loVkABipArxya; loVkamata; janasAmAnayxralilx rUDhiyAgiruva, (\kanmu\ neYtika parxshenxgaLanunx kurita) BAvane yA aBipArxya.
\num{5} (nidiRSaTx parxshenxya bagegx obabxna) AloVcane; daqDhABipArxya; daqDha naMbike: \eng{my opinion on smoking} dhUmapAnada bagegx nananx aBipArxya, AloVcane.
\num{6} (vAsatxvAMsha yA sariyAda karxma hiVgeMdu salahe keVLidAga niVDuva) tajAcnxBipArxya; tajacnx salahe; tajacnxna, pariNatana--vidhivatAtxda heVLike; vaqtitx nipuNana aBipArxya: \eng{you had better have another opinion} niVnu matotxbabx tajacnxna salaheyanunx paDeyuvudu meVlu.
\num{7} eNike; aBipArxya: \eng{have a very high opinion of him} avana bagegx nanage bahaLa oLeLxya aBipArxyavide.
\num{8} (niSeVdhapadadoDane) sadaBipArxya; oLeLxya aBipArxya; mecicxke toVrisuva aBipArxya: \eng{I have no opinion of Frenchmen} pherxMcf janara bagegx nanage oLeLxya aBipArxyavilalx.
\num{9} (\nAyxshA) kAraNa--nideRVsha, nirUpaNa; tiVpiRge AdhAravAda kAraNagaLanunx tiLisuva viduyxkatx heVLike.}}

naMbu.

\bentry

\bentry
\word{option}
\pron{ApaSxnf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} Ayekx; Ayuvudu.
\num{2} Ayadxdudx yA AyabahudAdadudx: \eng{make one's option} tananx
Ayekxyanunx mADu. 
\num{3} Ayekxya sAvxtaMtarxyX.
\num{4} (sarakArada sAlapatarx, patarx vAyxpAra kaTeTx, \mo vugaLa
\vi) gotAtxda baMDavALapatarx \mo vanunx gotAtxda kAladalilx, gotAtxda
belege, tarisikoLaLxlu yA baTavADe (pAvati) mADalu, haNakoTuTx paDeda
hakukx.}} 

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}

\bentry
\word[order(1)]{order}
\pron{ADaRrf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} sherxVNi; soVpAna; sAlu; paMkitx (Iga \viparx): \eng{order on
order of sculptured figures} sherxVNiya meVle sherxVNiyAgidadx
shilapxkaqtigaLu.
\num{2} sAmAjika vagaR, dajeR, aMtasutx: \eng{the higher orders}
meVladxjeRgaLu. 
\num{3} bage; taraha; parxkAra; riVti: \eng{talents of a high order}
unanxta maTaTxda sahaja shakitxgaLu. 
\num{4} (deVvatA)vagaR; `serAphimf', `cerubimf', \mo\ oMbatutx vagaRda
deVvategaLalilx yAvudeV vagaR. 
\num{5} (kerxYsatx pAdirxgaLa) vagaR; sherxVNi; dajeR; biSapf,
DiVkanf, \mo\ beVre beVre dajeRgaLalilx oMdu: \eng{(holy) orders}
pAdirx padavi, hudedx. 
\num{6} (mAMkfgaLu, pharxyarfgaLu matutx hiMde (kerxYsatx)
dhamaRviVraru, meVsanaru, \mo vara) vagaR; daLa; paMtha:
\eng{Franciscan order} saMta phAnisxsasxna vagaR, daLa, paMtha.
\num{7} (rAjaniMda birudu \mo vugaLanunx paDedu sanAmxtitarAdavara) 

\alnum{a} vagaR; sherxVNi: \eng{Order of the Garter} gATaRrf vagaR.

\alnum{b} iMtha vagaRdavara lAMCana: \eng{wears the order of the
Golden Fleece} `goVlaDxnf philxVSf' vagaRda lAMCanavanunx
dharisutAtxne. 
\num{8} (\vAshi) riVti; sheYli: \eng{five (classical) orders} aidu
aBijAta sheYligaLu (DoVrikf, ayAnikf, koriMtiyanf, Tasakxnf matutx
kAMposiTf).
\quad\hyperlink{orders-8figure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage
    width 0.6cm height 0.4cm {O_Pictures/orders-8.jpg}}}
\num{9} (\ga) dajeR:

\alnum{a} yAvudeV biVjagaNitoVkitxyalilxruva padagaLalilx kANabaruva
atuyxnanxta GAta: $\left(ax^2+bx+c\right)$ \eng{is an equation of the
second order}. $\left(ax^2+bx+c\right)$ eMbudu eraDane dajeRya
gaNitoVkitx.

\alnum{b} (yAvudeV motatxda parxmANavanunx nideRVshisuva) dajeR;
maTaTx: \eng{the wavelength of visible light is of the order of
thousand angstroms} daqshayx beLakina aleyudadx halavu sAvira
AYxMgfsATxrXmfgaLa dajeRyadu. 
\num{10} (\jiVvi) gaNa; pArxNigaLa vagiRVkaraNadalilx vagaRkikxMta
keLaginadu matutx vaMshakikxMta meVlinadu.
\num{11} (\sA\ $10$ra guNada, gAtarxda AdhArada meVle vagiRVkarisida
padadhxti yA vayxvasethxyalilxna) vagaR: \eng{order of magnitude}
gAtarxda AdhArada meVle, \sA\ $10$ra GAtada AdhArada meVle,
vagiRVkarisalAguva padadhxtiya oMdu vagaR.
\num{12} karxma; anukarxma: \eng{alphabetical order} akArAdi karxma. 
\num{13} vayxvasithxta karxma; vayxvasethx; parxtiyoMdu aMsha, BAga,
\mo vu tamamx ucita sAthxnadalilxruva sithxti: \eng{love of order}
(utatxma) vayxvasethxya perxVma.
\num{14} (\birx) (\pArxparx) kAyaRkarxma; vidhAna: \eng{take order to
do} (yAvudanenxV) mADalu (agatayxvAda) kAyaRkarxmavanunx anusarisu.
\num{15} jagatutx, samAja, \mo vugaLa savxrUpa yA vayxvasethx, karxma:
\eng{the moral order of the world} jagatitxna neYtika vayxvasethx.
\num{16} (shAsanasaBe \mo vugaLalilx anusarisabeVkAda niyamAvaLigaLu,
kAyaRvidhAna, \mo vugaLa) shisutx; karxma; paripATa; riVti:
\eng{Order! Order!} shisutx! shisutx!.
\num{17} shAMtivayxvasethx; shAMti (parisithxti); galaBe, goMdalagaLu
ilalxde, kAnUnugaLanunx pAlane mADutatx iruva sithxti: \eng{law and
order} shAMta sithxti; shAsana badadhx vayxvasethx; shAMti: \eng{law
and order was restored} shAMtiyanunx punaH sAthxpisalAyitu. \eng{keep
order} shAMti (sithxti) pAlisi.
\num{18} (seYnayx) sAlu; paMkitx; sherxVNi; seYnikaranunx joVDisiruva
karxma: \eng{open order} tereda sAlu; viraLa sAlu; seYnika--seYnikara
naDuve aMtaraviruvaMte nililxsida seYnikara sAlu. \eng{close order}
mucicxda sAlu; otutx sAlu; seYnikarelalx otAtxgi, naDuve aMtara
ilalxde nilulxva sAlu.
\num{19} (\bava dalilx saha) kaTuTxpADu; kaTaTxLe; apapxNe; Ajecnx;
AdeVsha; hukumu: \eng{gave orders} apapxNe, --koTaTx. \eng{till
further orders} muMdina AdeVshadavarege.
\num{20} (bAyxMkiMgf \mo vugaLa) nideRVsha; sUcane.
\num{21} (vANijayx) 

\alnum{a} koVrike; nideRVsha; sUcane; ADaRru; vAyxpArigoV
tayArakanigoV yAvudeV sarakanunx sarabarAju mADuvaMte kaLuhisida
sUcane.

\alnum{b} hAge odagisida saraku \mo vugaLa motatx. 
\num{22} (nATaka yA saMgiVta shAle, mUyxsiyamf, KAsagi mane, \mo
vugaLige shulakxrahitavAgi yA alapx shulakxkekx yA oMdu hakAkxgi,
parxveVshisalu koDuva) parxveVshapatarx; apapxNe ciVTi; pAsu.
\num{23} (\kerxY) dhAmiRka vidhi; vidhuyxkatxvAda kamaRvidhAna:
\eng{the order of confirmation} (jAcnxnasAnxnavAdavarige niVDuva)
sithxriVkaraNa saMsAkxra vidhi.}}

\bentry
\word[ornament(1)]{ornament}
\pron{AnaRmaMTf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (cacuR) (\sA\ \bava dalilx) pUjA sAdhanagaLu; pUjoVpakaraNagaLu (\udA\ balipiVTha, baTaTxlu, pAterxgaLu, pavitarx garxMthagaLu, \mo vu).
\num{2} (\saM) (\bava dalilx) alaMkAra (savxra)gaLu; gAyanada yA vAdanada sobaganunx hecicxsalu gAyakanu yA vAdakanu racisuva, camatAkxradiMda kUDida, savxra yoVjanegaLu.
\num{3} (\Eva dalilx mAtarx) alaMkAra; siMgAra: \eng{a tower rich in ornament} alaMkAragaLiMda shirxVmaMtavAgiruva goVpura; alaMkAra siriyuLaLx goVpura.
\num{4} ABaraNa; oDave; alaMkArakAkxgi baLasuva vasutx, \kanmu\ thaLuku paLukina oDave \mo vu: \eng{her only ornament was a brooch} avaLa EkeYka oDaveyeMdare borxVcu.
\num{5} BUSaNa; BUSaNapArxya vayxkitx yA alaMkArapArxya guNa;
aMdagoLisuva, gwrava \mo vanunx taruva--guNa yA vayxkitx: \eng{an ornament to her profession} avaLa vaqtitxge oMdu BUSaNa.}}

\bentry
\word[other(1)]{other}
\pron{adarf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} beVrobabx yA beVroMdu; inonxMdu yA inonxbabx;
matotxMdu yA matotxbabx; anayx; itara; para; beVre; IgAgaleV
heVLidadxlalxda yA sUcisidadxlalxda; vayxkitx yA jAtiyalilx
BinanxvAda: \eng{other people} beVreyavaru; itara jana. \eng{other
means} beVre sAdhana; Binanx mAgaR. \eng{my reason is quite other}
nananx kAraNa tiVra beVreyAdudu.
\num{2} adhika; hecicxna; beVre; matetx; jotege: \eng{we have other
evidence} namamxlilx beVre (hecicxna) sAkaSxyXvide. \eng{a few other
examples} matetx kelavu udAharaNegaLu.
\num{3} eraDaralilx oMdu yA ibabxralilx obabx: \eng{open your other
eye} ninanx inonxMdu kaNuNx tere.
\num{4} (\eng{the} oDane) uLida; mikakx; parxsakatxvAdudanunx biTuTx
itara elalxvanUnx parigaNisida, nirAkarisida, \mo\ taruvAya uLiyuva:
\eng{must be in the other pocket} inonxMdu jiVbinalilxrabeVku.
\eng{where are the other two}? uLidibabxru yA mikikxbabxru elilx? 
\num{5} (\eng{than} jotege) vinA; biTuTx; horatu; uLidu: \eng{any
person other than you} ninanxnunx biTuTx yAvanAdarU.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{an other two}

\alnum{a} beVre eraDu.

\alnum{b} matetx eraDu.
\num{2} \eng{every other day} dinabiTuTx dina; parxti marudina:
\eng{happens every other day} parxti marudina saMBavisutatxde.
\num{3} \eng{no (\engit{or} none) other than} beVre yArU yA yAvudU alalx:
\eng{it was none other than Ram} adu beVre yArU Agirade, savxyaM
rAmaneV Agidadx.
\num{4} \eng{on the other hand} (hiMdinadakekx virudadhxvAda yA
vayxtAyxsavAda saMgatiyanunx yA vAdavanunx muMdiDuvAga \parx)
sariyAgi noVDidare; inonxMdu kaDeyalilx; matotxMdu saMdaBaR
yoVcisidare.
\num{5} \eng{other things being equal} mikakx viSayagaLu samavAgidudx
yA samavAgidadxre.
\num{6} \eng{somehow or other} heVgoV; heVgAdarU; yAvudeV riVtiyalilx.
\num{7} \eng{some one or other} yArAdarU; yAvanAdarU obabx: \eng{some
idiots or other have been shouting all night hoarse} yAroV
aviveVkigaLu rAtirxyelAlx bobebx hAkutitxdadxru.
\num{8} \eng{something or other} yAvudAdarU oMdu.
\num{9} \eng{some time or other} eMdAdarU, oMdalalx oMdu dina.
\num{10} \eng{some way or other} yAvudAdarU, yAvudoV oMdu --
riVtiyalilx.
\num{11} \eng{the other thing} (\kanmu\ hAsayx \parx) (sapxSaTxvAgi
adanunx heVLadiruvAga) A inonxMdu: \eng{if you don't like it, do the
other thing} ninage adu hiDisadidadxre, A inonxMdanunx mADu.
\num{12} \eng{the other day(\engit{or} night or week etc.,)} aMdu; Avatutx;
kelavu dinagaLa hiMde; ititxVcege; monenxmonenx.
\num{13} \eng{the other two} (anidiRSaTxvAgi heVLuvAga \parx)
mikikxbabxru; uLideraDu.
\num{14} \eng{the other woman} A inonxbabx heMgasu; vivAhitana
upapatinx, nalelx.
\num{15} \eng{the other world} paraloVka.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[other(2)]{other}
\pron{adarf}
\gl{\nA (athavA \sanA)}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} inonxMdu; beVreyadu; inonxbabx; beVrobabx; beVre riVtiyadu:
\eng{give me one other (\engit{or} another)} nanage beVreyadanunx yA
beVroMdanunx koDu. 
\eng{do good to others} pararige oLeLxyadanunx mADu.
\num{2} (\bava dalilx \eng{the} oDane) uLida, mikakx--vayxkitx yA
vasutx: \eng{where are the others} mikakxvarelilx?}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{I can do no other} (\pArxparx) nAnu beVre
EnanUnx mADalAre.
\num{2} \eng{in other of} mikakx uLida: \eng{in other of his sermons}
avana uLida parxvacanagaLalilx.
\num{3} \eng{of all others} elalxralilx; elalxdaralilx: \eng{on this
night of all others} elalx rAtirxgaLalilx I rAtirx.}

\bentry
\word[out(1)]{out}
\pron{auTf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} horage; horagaDe; Ace; horakekx; horagaDege; Acege:
\eng{he is out} avanu (maneyiMda) horage hoVgidAdxne. \eng{keep him
out} avananunx horagiDu. \eng{turn him out} avananunx horakekx
aTuTx. \eng{get out of here} ililxMda horakekx hoVgu.
\eng{my son is out in Canada} nananx maga kenaDAdalilx idAdxne.
\num{2} (\pagu da \kirx gaLanunx rUpisuvAga) 

\alnum{a} oMdu sathxLa \mo vugaLiMda cedari hoVguvudanunx
sUcisuvalilx: \eng{hire out } bADigege tegedukoMDu hoVgu. \eng{board
out} beVre kaDe hoVgi UTa mADu.

\alnum{b} sAvaRjanikara gamana \mo vugaLige baruvudu yA taruvudanunx
sUcisalu: \eng{call out}

\quad{\rm\phantom{ii}(i)} kUgu; GoVSisu.

\quad{\rm\phantom{i}(ii)} kUgi kare.

\quad{\rm(iii)} lakaSxyXviDabeVkAda Avashayxkateyanunx sUcisalu:
\eng{watch out} gamanisu. \eng{look out} noVDu.
\num{3} horage; horagaDe; mane, kaceVri, \mo\ kaDegaLalilx ilalxde:
\eng{went out for a walk} horagaDe naDagege hoVdaru. 
\eng{she has her Sundays out} avaLu BAnuvAragaLanunx maneyiMda horage
kaLeyutAtxLe.
\num{4} pUNaRvAgi; pUtiR(yAgi); mugiyuvavarege; konetanaka: \eng{she
had her cry out} Ake (tananx duHKavelalx mugiyuvavaregU) pUtiRyAgi
atutx biTaTxLu, aLuvaSuTx atutx mugisidaLu. \eng{tried out}
(shakitxyelalx mugidu hoVguvaSuTx) pUtiR AyAsavAgiru; basavaLidiru;
susAtxgi hoVgiru. \eng{die out} pUtiR aLidu hoVgu. \eng{fight it out}
kone tanaka hoVrADu. \eng{typed it out} pUtiR beraLacucx mADida.
\num{5} (beMki, moVMbatitx, \mo vugaLa \vi) Ari; naMdi; uriyade.
\num{6} (lekAkxcAra, aMdAju, niriVkaSxNe) tapATxgi: \eng{I was out in
my calculations} nananx lekAkxcAravelalx, niriVkaSxNeyelalx tapApxgi
hoVyitu. 
\num{7} (\AmA) parxjecnxyilalxde; mUCeR hoVgi; jAcnxna tapipx:
\eng{she was out for five minutes} avaLu aidu nimiSa mUCeR
hoVgidadxLu.
\num{8} 
\alnum{a} (halilxna \vi) kitutx; tegedu hAki.

\alnum{b} (kiVlu, mULe, \mo vugaLa \vi) kiVlu tapipx; sAthxna
palalxTavAgi: \eng{his arm is out} avana toVLu kiVlu tapipx
hoVgide. \eng{put his shoulder out} Buja sAthxnapalalxTavAyitu.
\num{9} (oMdu pakaSx, rAjakAraNi, \mo vara \vi) padavi, adhikAra --
kaLedukoMDu: \eng{the Tories are out} ToVrigaLu adhikAra
kaLedukoMDidAdxre.
\num{10} (jUri yA nAyxyadashiRgaLa \vi) tamamx tiVpaRnunx goVpayxvAgi
parishiVlisutatx.
\num{11} (kelasagArara \vi) kelasa biTuTx; caLuvaLi mADutAtx; muSakxra
hUDi; haratALadalilx: \eng{miners are out} gaNigAraru muSakxra
hUDidADxre.
\num{12} (guTiTxna \vi) horakekx; bayalige; bahiraMgakekx; beLakige:
\eng{the secret is out} guTuTx bayalige baMdide.
\num{13} (hUvina \vi) araLi; biridu; vikasisi: \eng{the rose is out}
gulAbi araLide.
\num{14} (pusatxkada \vi) parxkaTanagoMDu; parxkAshakekx,
beLakige--baMdu; hora baMdu: \eng{the book is out} pusatxka hora
bididxde. 
\num{15} (nakaSxtarxda \vi) (katatxleyAda naMtara) kANisutatx;
goVcaravAgi.
\num{16} baLake, rUDhi, vADike, phAYxSanf--tapipx: \eng{crinolines
are out} kirxnolinf baTeTxgaLu phAyxSanf tapipxhoVgive.
\num{17} (bAyxTugAra \mo vara \vi) 

\alnum{a} (kAYxcf koTuTx saTxMpf Agi, \mo\ kAraNadiMda) horakekx;
vikeTf kaLedukoMDu; auTAgi: \eng{the batsman is out} bAYxTugAranu
auTAgidAdxne, vikeTanunx kaLedukoMDidAdxne. \eng{all out} elalxrU, oMdu
kaDeya bAYxTugArarelalxrU, auTf AgidAdxre.

tiVpuR. \eng{not out} auTilalx; auTAgilalx; bAYxTugAranu auTf
AgilalxveMdu aMpeYrf koDuva tiVpuR.
\num{18} parigaNanege yoVgayxvAgirade; tirasakxrisalapxTuTx: \eng{that
idea is out} A BAvane tirasakxrisalapxTiTxde.
\num{19} (\AmA) (tamarUpada taruvAya \parx) ideyeMdu gotAtxgi:
\eng{the best game out} atuyxtatxma ATavAgideyeMdu gotAtxgi.
\num{20} (kale, gurutu, \mo vugaLa \vi) kANadaMtAgisi; tegedu hAki:

gamanakekx baMdide.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}

\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{horaharita; hora parxvAha; bahiHparxvAha; 
niHsArxva:

\alnum{a} horagaDege hariyuvudu.

\alnum{b} horage hariduhoVguva parxmANa.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{outflux}

\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} horaharivu; bahisAsxrXva; bahiHparxvAha.
\num{2} bahiHsarxvaNa sAthxna; horakekx suriyuva sAthxna.
\num{3} (nadi \mo vugaLa) muKa; avu samudarx \mo vanunx seVruva jAga.
\num{4} horakekx hariyuva parxmANa; horaharivu, bahisAsxrXva, bahiH 
sarxvaNa-parxmANa.}
\eentry

\bentry

sound} hAruvudaralilx dhavxniya veVgavanunx miVrisu;
shabadxveVgavanunx miVrihAru.}

\num{2} (keYbiTuTx) horage hoVda haNa; (horage) hoVdadudx; KacuR; vayxya; vecacx: \eng{a record of income and outgo} Ayavayxyada dAKale.

\num{2} (yAvudanenxV) kAnUnuvirudadhxveMdu sAru, GoVSisu;
kAnUnubAhiragoLisu; shAsanabAhira mADu: \eng{the $18$th Amendment
outlawed the manufacture and sale of liquor in the U.S.A} $18$neya
tidudxpaDi amerikada saMyukatx saMsAthxnadalilx madayxda tayArike,
mArATagaLanunx shAsanabAhiragoLisitu. 
\num{3} niSeVdhisu; taDehAku: \eng{outlaw smoking in a theatre} nATaka
yA sinimA maMdiradalilx taMbAku seVduvudanunx niSeVdhisu.}

hecicxna parxmANa: \eng{a hundred people at the outside} paramAvadhi

\bentry
\word{overbear}
\pron{OvarfbeVrf}
\gl{\sakirx} (\BU\ \eng{overbore}, \BUkaq\ \eng{overborne}).
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} hecucx BAra yA balaparxyoVgadiMda (edurALiyanunx) uruLisi biDu, soVlisi biDu: \eng{with his superior strength he easily overbore his opponent in the fight} tananx hecucx baladiMda avanu tananx edurALiyanunx kALagadalilx sarAgavAgi uruLisibiTaTx.
\num{2} balAtAkxradiMda yA adhikArabaladiMda--adumu, meTuTx, tuLi.
\num{3} (beVrobabxra bayakegaLu, AkeSxVpagaLu, \mo vanunx) taLiLxhAku; badi gotutx: \eng{he overbore all objections to his plan} tananx yoVjaneya meVlaNa AkeSxVpagaLanenxlalx avanu taLiLxhAkida.
\num{4} ati dapaRdiMda vatiRsu: \eng{he overbears his children with threats of punishment} shikeSxya bedarikegaLanunx hAki tananx makakxLoDane avanu ati dapaRdiMda vatiRsutAtxne.
\num{5} (pArxmuKayx, parxBAva, \mo vugaLalilx) miVrisu; meVlAgu.}

\bentry
\word[override(1)]{override}
\pron{OvareYDf}
\gl{\sakirx} (\BU\ \eng{overrode}, \BUkaq\ \eng{overridden}).
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kudureyanunx) atiyAgi savAri mADi baLalisu.
\num{2} (sajijxta seYnayxdiMda) shaturxdeVshada meVlAvxyudx hoVgu; shaturxdeVshada meVle dALi mADu.
\num{3} (vayxkitxyanunx) kudureya kAlinaDiyalilx tuLisu.
\num{4} (\rUpa) tuLidu hAku; (itarara salaheyanunx yA aBipArxyavanunx
badigotitx) tananx saMkalapxvanunx yA adhikAravanunx (avara meVle)
heVru: \eng{override one's advisers} (samAloVcakara salaheyanunx
taLiLx hAki) sevxVceCxyanenxV naDesu.
\num{5} beVrobabx adhikAriya tiVmARnavanunx radudxpaDisu:
\eng{override all previous decisions} hiMdina tiVmARnagaLanenxlalx
radudxpaDisu.
\num{6} (\shaveY) adhikarxmisu; (\sA\ murida mULeya oMdu tuMDina \vi)
inonxMdara meVle kUru, sari, cAcu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[overrun(1)]{overrun}
\pron{Ovaranf}
\gl{\sakirx} (\vakaq\ \eng{overrunning}; \BU\ \eng{overran}; \BUkaq\ adeV).
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (nelavanunx) parxvAhadalilx muLugisu; (nelada meVle) parxvAha harisu.
\num{2} (oMdu deVsha, parxdeVsha, \mo vugaLa meVle) apapxNeyilalxde hAdu hoVgu.
\num{3} (oMdu deVshada meVle) daMDu nugigxsu; dALi mADu.
\num{4} (oMdu deVshavanunx) sadebaDi; dhavxMsa mADu.
\num{5} (huLugaLu, kirxmikiVTagaLu, kaLegaLu, kADu giDagaLu, \mo vugaLa \vi) oMdara meVle atiyAgi--haraDu, habubx.
\num{6} (\rUpa) (BAvane, naMbike, \mo vugaLa \vi) atiyAgi habibxko; vipariVta parxcAragoLuLx.
\num{7} (mudarxNa)

\alnum{a} sAlanunx matetx joVDisu; paMkitxyalilx akaSxragaLanunx seVrisidadxriMda yA tegeduhAkidadxriMda uMTAda joVDaNeyaMte paMkitxyanunx kUDisiko, punarf vayxvasethx mADu.

\alnum{b} (pusatxka, keYpiDi, hasatxpatirxke, \mo vanunx) adhika
parxti, hecucx parxti mudirxsu; apapxNe mADidadxkikxMta hecucx parxmANadalilx, saMKeyxyalilx mudirxsu.

\alnum{c} (pada \mo vanunx) muMdina sAlu yA muMdina puTadalilx muMduvarisu.
\num{8} mitiyanonxV gaDukAlavanonxV--miVru.
\num{9} (\yaMshA) (inonxMdakikxMta) veVgavAgi sututx, tirugu.}
\eentry

\bentry

\num{3} (vimAnada \vi) (iLidANadalilx iLiyuvAga yA EruvAga) OTada hAdiya Acege hAru yA OTada hAdiyalilx bahaLa dUra ODu.}}

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) guri mIru; udedxVshavanunx yA ucitavAdudanunx mIri hoVgu; ati dUra hoVgu.

\alnum{c} (vayxkitx, saMdaBaR, \mo vanunx) tapApxgi garxhisi tapupx mADu.
\num{2} \eng{overshoot oneself}

\alnum{a} guri mIri hoDe; guriyAcege hoDeyuva mUlaka guri tapupx.

\alnum{b} utepxrXVkiSxsu; atishayisu.

\alnum{c} (tananx udedxVshakekx yA hitakekx) dhakekxyAguvaSuTx dUra hoVgu, tapipxge biVLu.}
